function view__id1__id2_cbMain__id135__id378_clientSide_onclick(thisEvent) {
// verify that at least one language and file type are selected
var vLangChk = false;
var langFld = document.getElementsByName("view:_id1:_id2:cbMain:_id135:cbDlgLangs");
for ( var l = 0; l < langFld.length; l++) {
	if (langFld[l].checked) {
		vLangChk = true;
		break;
	};
};

var vFileChk = false;
var fileFld = document.getElementsByName("view:_id1:_id2:cbMain:_id135:cbDlgFiles");
for ( var f = 0; f < fileFld.length; f++) {
	if (fileFld[f].checked) {
		vFileChk = true;
		break;
	};
};

if (!vLangChk || !vFileChk) {
	alert("Please select at least one language and at least one file type");
	return false;
};

return true;

}
